Send Owasp-greece mailing list submissions to
        owasp-greece at lists.owasp.org

To subscribe or unsubscribe via the World Wide Web, visit
        https://lists.owasp.org/mailman/listinfo/owasp-greece
or, via email, send a message with subject or body 'help' to
        owasp-greece-request at lists.owasp.org

You can reach the person managing the list at
        owasp-greece-owner at lists.owasp.org

When replying, please edit your Subject line so it is more specific
than "Re: Contents of Owasp-greece digest..."

kanei, an uparxei akoma :-).

Kata deutero giati leei sto mail?
